GT Equivalence Verification (PO19)

GT: -c0*beta*v - omega0**c1*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

Looking at the GT: `-0.59954989233168*v - 2.79522534599104*x*exp(-Abs(x))`

The key challenge is matching the term `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. Let me analyze this function's behavior:

For x > 0: `x*exp(-x)` — this starts at 0, peaks around x=1, then decays exponentially.
For x < 0: `x*exp(x)` — this is an odd function reflection.

The function `x*exp(-|x|)` is an odd function of x.

**Can any polynomial/rational/piecewise combination match `x*exp(-|x|)`?**

No finite polynomial can equal `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x. So I need candidates that contain exponential or similar transcendental terms.

Let me check candidates with `exp(c*x)` terms. The issue is that `exp(-|x|)` is NOT `exp(cx)` for any constant c, since `exp(-|x|)` behaves differently for positive and negative x. So `c1*exp(c2*x)` cannot reproduce `exp(-|x|)`.

Candidates with `x*Abs(x)` — this equals `x²*sign(x)`, which is NOT `x*exp(-|x|)`.

Candidates with `x*cos(c*x)` — this is oscillatory, not matching the exponential decay.

Candidates with `x/(c*x² + 1)` — Let me check if this could approximate `x*exp(-|x|)`. These are rational functions, not equal to `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x.

Candidates with `x*log(c*x² + 1)` — also not equivalent.

Candidate 11: `c0*x + c1*v + c2*x**3 + c3*v*x**2 + c4*x**5 + c5*v**3 + c6*x*cos(c7*x) + c8*x*Abs(x)**c9`

The term `c8*x*Abs(x)**c9` — if we could choose c9 such that `x*|x|^c9 = x*exp(-|x|)` for all x, that would require `|x|^c9 = exp(-|x|)` for all x, which is impossible since the left side is a power function and the right is exponential.

Candidate 12: `c0*x**c1 + c2*v*sin(c3*x + c4) + c5*x + c6*v + c7*x**3 + c8*x*Abs(x)`

The `x**c1` term — this is a single power, can't match `x*exp(-|x|)`.

Candidate 41: `c0*x**2 + c1*x + c2 + c3*exp(c4*x) + c5*v + c6*x**c7`

Again, `exp(c4*x)` is one-sided exponential, and `x**c7` is a power — neither matches `x*exp(-|x|)`.

Candidate 36: `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*v*x**2 + c3*x + c4 + c5*v + c6*v**2*x + c7*x*Abs(x)**c8`

The term `x*|x|^c8` — same issue as above.

**None of these candidates contain a term that can reproduce `x*exp(-|x|)`.**

The fundamental issue is that `x*exp(-|x|)` is a transcendental function that:
1. Cannot be represented by any polynomial
2. Cannot be represented by `exp(cx)` (which is one-sided)
3. Cannot be represented by rational functions like `x/(cx²+1)`
4. Cannot be represented by `x*|x|^c` (power functions)
5. Cannot be represented by trigonometric functions

None of the candidate formulas contain the structural form needed to exactly match `x*exp(-|x|)` for all x.

- For x < 0: x*exp(x)
- It's an odd function (antisymmetric)
- It's NOT a polynomial, NOT a rational function, NOT expressible as finite combinations of polynomials, x*|x|, trig functions, etc.

**Key insight:** `x*exp(-|x|)` cannot be exactly represented by:
- Polynomials (x, x², x³, x⁵, etc.)
- x*|x| (which is x²*sign(x))
- x*cos(cx) for any fixed c
- Rational functions like x/(cx²+1)
- x*log(cx²+1)
- Finite sums of the above
